2025-05-24 18:30:12.339 +05:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (6ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [c].[Name] AS [Category], [s].[Name] AS [Supplier], [m].[Price], [m].[Quantity], [m].[ExpiryDate], [m].[Description]
FROM [Medicines] AS [m]
